          function selecionaTipoConteudoParaBuscaTextual() {
              //zera o que estiver marcado
              $("#searchBar .options input[type=radio]").removeAttr("checked");
              var inputRadioId = "#type-" + $("#nav").find(".on").attr("id")

              if($(inputRadioId).length > 0){
                $(inputRadioId).attr("checked", true);
              } else {
                  //default perguntas
                $("#type-nav_questions").attr("checked", true);
              }
          }
          $(document).ready(function() {
            selecionaTipoConteudoParaBuscaTextual();
          });

    var realtime = function(realtimeLoaded, msg){
        if(realtimeLoaded){
            return;
        }

        $.getScript('http://s.glbimg.com/bu/rt/js/glb-rt.js', function(){
            $.ajax({
                dataType: 'jsonp',
                
                url: 'http://s.glbimg.com/es/ge/static/live/globoesporte/json/globoesporte-home-agregador.js',
                
                jsonpCallback: 'glbrealtime_callback',
                cache: true,
                success: function(json){
                    $.glbrealtime({
                        data: json,
                        debug: false
                    });
                }
            });
        });
    }

    var realtimeLoaded = false;

    $(window).on('load', function(){
        realtime(realtimeLoaded, "onLoad");
        realtimeLoaded = true;
    })

    setTimeout(function(){
        realtime(realtimeLoaded, "timeout")
        realtimeLoaded = true;
    }, 3000);
